000059sec-overview Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_269e2f88-6bfa-cbc3-777c-ea257bf1ae36" anchor="sec-overview" obligation="normative">
<title>Overview</title>
<clause id="_7974148b-49a2-46ca-9056-19844c611e4e" obligation="normative">
<title>Introduction</title>
<p id="_fc88f2b0-df1f-e39e-2483-04f6a4e18697">S-411 is the Ice Information Product Specification, produced by the World Meteorological Organization (WMO)/Intergovernmental Oceanographic Commission Technical Commission for Oceanography and Marine Meteorology (JCOMM) Expert Team on Sea Ice (ETSI).<br/> This document has been produced in response to a requirement to produce a data product that can be used as an Information Overlay within an Electronic Chart Display and Information Systems (ECDIS). It is based on the IHO S-100 framework specification, the ISO 19100 series of standards and Geography Markup Language (GML). It is a vector product specification that is intended for encoding the extent and nature of Sea Ice for navigational purpose in ice covered regions.</p>
2

001237_d150c197-58f5-c38b-9100-71261317f2d6 Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_d150c197-58f5-c38b-9100-71261317f2d6" obligation="normative">
<title>Application Schema</title>
<p id="_a933ab53-c2f9-53de-7d84-6a36cbef5be3">S-411 conforms to the General Feature Model (GFM) from S-100 Part 3. The GFM is the conceptual model and the implementation is defined in the Feature Catalogue which is included as a separate Annex (Annex C) and provides a full specification of all types including feature types, their attributes, allowed and values. The S-411 Product Specification only contains specific examples.</p>

<p id="_2d11f645-63d2-8d75-27d2-eee5ebacb9ad">The following conventions are used in the UML diagrams depicting the application schema:</p>

001720sec-data-quality Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_c1860425-312b-4dbc-5238-484edadcae2b" anchor="sec-data-quality" obligation="normative">
<title>Data Quality</title>
<p id="_730a5683-2034-ab8f-8c53-9b48e13197bb">As ice charts are done for different purposes (from weekly overview to tactical charts and further to model forecasts) data quality can differ.</p>

<p id="_99dac53a-3244-d6f2-42a7-87afc798a5c0">Differences can also be found between ice charts of the same region and same nominal date resulting from different issuing agencies or also from different forecasts models.</p>
2
001808sec-portrayal Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_06ac00cd-1656-81b8-a081-262a9d3c2d71" anchor="sec-portrayal" obligation="normative">
<title>Portrayal</title>
<clause id="_0430ff1e-3416-9d49-46fa-0fecc2b34a2a" obligation="normative">
<title>Rules</title>
<p id="_cc8f3414-e780-ff59-8d8a-68de295de356" anchor="fig-portrayal-rules"> <tt>main.xsl</tt> includes all the rules for single feature types. It manages the selection of the right rule, depending on current feature type in <tt>dataset and parameters in `iceDisplayParameters.xml</tt>.</p>

003098subsec-s100_​exchangecatalo­gue Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="_c6c763c7-293b-a50f-f07a-88c99d6584c0" anchor="subsec-s100_exchangecatalogue" obligation="normative">
<title>S100_ExchangeCatalogue</title>
<p id="_5338d7c9-d529-fdfb-2fa8-001a70dd9ab1">Each Exchange Set has a single S100_ExchangeCatalogue which contains meta information for the data in the Exchange Set.</p>

<p id="_b04ad31c-c4e3-db7a-edee-0a30d3e49321">S-411 uses S100_ExchangeCatalogue without modification.</p>
